\documentclass{article}\usepackage[]{graphicx}\usepackage[]{color}
%% maxwidth is the original width if it is less than linewidth
%% otherwise use linewidth (to make sure the graphics do not exceed the margin)
\makeatletter
\def\maxwidth{ %
  \ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth
    \linewidth
  \else
    \Gin@nat@width
  \fi
}
\makeatother

\definecolor{fgcolor}{rgb}{0.345, 0.345, 0.345}
\newcommand{\hlnum}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.686,0.059,0.569}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstr}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.192,0.494,0.8}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlcom}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.678,0.584,0.686}{\textit{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlopt}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0,0,0}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.345,0.345,0.345}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwa}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.161,0.373,0.58}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwb}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.69,0.353,0.396}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwc}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.333,0.667,0.333}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.737,0.353,0.396}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\let\hlipl\hlkwb

\usepackage{framed}
\makeatletter
\newenvironment{kframe}{%
 \def\at@end@of@kframe{}%
 \ifinner\ifhmode%
  \def\at@end@of@kframe{\end{minipage}}%
  \begin{minipage}{\columnwidth}%
 \fi\fi%
 \def\FrameCommand##1{\hskip\@totalleftmargin \hskip-\fboxsep
 \colorbox{shadecolor}{##1}\hskip-\fboxsep
     % There is no \\@totalrightmargin, so:
     \hskip-\linewidth \hskip-\@totalleftmargin \hskip\columnwidth}%
 \MakeFramed {\advance\hsize-\width
   \@totalleftmargin\z@ \linewidth\hsize
   \@setminipage}}%
 {\par\unskip\endMakeFramed%
 \at@end@of@kframe}
\makeatother

\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{.97, .97, .97}
\definecolor{messagecolor}{rgb}{0, 0, 0}
\definecolor{warningcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 1}
\definecolor{errorcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 0}
\newenvironment{knitrout}{}{} % an empty environment to be redefined in TeX

\usepackage{alltt}

\usepackage{listings}
\usepackage{MnSymbol}

\lstset{prebreak=\raisebox{0ex}[0ex][0ex]
        {\ensuremath{\rhookswarrow}}}
\lstset{postbreak=\raisebox{0ex}[0ex][0ex]
        {\ensuremath{\rcurvearrowse\space}}}
\lstset{breaklines=true, breakatwhitespace=true}
\lstset{numbers=left, numberstyle=\scriptsize}
\IfFileExists{upquote.sty}{\usepackage{upquote}}{}
\begin{document}

\section{Importar taules}
Primer importem el diccionari de noms antics i nous:
\begin{knitrout}
\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{0.969, 0.969, 0.969}\color{fgcolor}\begin{kframe}
\begin{alltt}
\hlstd{rosetta} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{read.table}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"/home/lucas/ISGlobal/Gen_Referencies/Gene_references_rosetta.txt"}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fill} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fileEncoding} \hlstd{=} \hlstr{"UTF-8"}\hlstd{)}
\end{alltt}
\end{kframe}
\end{knitrout}
Després la llista de gens amb màxima differència segons transcripció:
\begin{knitrout}
\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{0.969, 0.969, 0.969}\color{fgcolor}\begin{kframe}
\begin{alltt}
\hlstd{diff_trans} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{read.table}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"/home/lucas/ISGlobal/Llista_diff_10G_12B.txt"}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fill} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fileEncoding} \hlstd{=} \hlstr{"UTF-8"}\hlstd{)}
\end{alltt}
\end{kframe}
\end{knitrout}

\begin{knitrout}
\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{0.969, 0.969, 0.969}\color{fgcolor}\begin{kframe}
\begin{alltt}
\hlcom{# alguna diferència segons transcripció}
\hlstd{diff_trans_all} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{read.table}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"/home/lucas/ISGlobal/Llista_diff_10G_12B_all.txt"}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fill} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fileEncoding} \hlstd{=} \hlstr{"UTF-8"}\hlstd{)}

\hlcom{# Differetial peak calling 10G}
\hlstd{diff_10G_met} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{read.table}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"/home/lucas/ISGlobal/metil_diff_10G_12B.txt"}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fill} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fileEncoding} \hlstd{=} \hlstr{"UTF-8"}\hlstd{)}
\hlstd{diff_10G_met} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{gsub}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"ID="}\hlstd{,} \hlstr{""}\hlstd{, diff_10G_met[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],} \hlkwc{fixed} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{)}

\hlcom{# Differential peak calling 1.2B}
\hlstd{diff_12B_met} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{read.table}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"/home/lucas/ISGlobal/metil_diff_12B_10G.txt"}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fill} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{,} \hlkwc{fileEncoding} \hlstd{=} \hlstr{"UTF-8"}\hlstd{)}
\hlstd{diff_12B_met} \hlkwb{<-} \hlkwd{gsub}\hlstd{(}\hlstr{"ID="}\hlstd{,} \hlstr{""}\hlstd{, diff_12B_met[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],} \hlkwc{fixed} \hlstd{=} \hlnum{TRUE}\hlstd{)}

\hlcom{#Comprovant que tots surten al diccionari}
\hlstd{diff_10G_met} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
\end{alltt}
\begin{verbatim}
##  [1]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
## [12]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
## [23]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE FALSE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
## [34]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE FALSE  TRUE  TRUE
## [45]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
## [56]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
## [67]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
## [78]  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE  TRUE
\end{verbatim}
\begin{alltt}
\hlstd{diff_trans[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{3}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{|} \hlstd{diff_trans[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{4}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{|} \hlstd{diff_trans[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{5}\hlstd{]}
\end{alltt}
\begin{verbatim}
##  [1] TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE
## [15] TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE
## [29] TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE
## [43] TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE TRUE
\end{verbatim}
\begin{alltt}
\hlcom{#### Traduïr tots els gens de "diff_trans" ####}
\hlkwa{for} \hlstd{(i} \hlkwa{in} \hlnum{1}\hlopt{:}\hlkwd{length}\hlstd{(diff_trans[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]))\{}
  \hlkwa{if} \hlstd{(diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{3}\hlstd{])\{}
    \hlstd{diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlkwb{<-} \hlstd{rosetta[rosetta[,}\hlnum{3}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
  \hlstd{\}} \hlkwa{else if} \hlstd{(diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{4}\hlstd{])\{}
    \hlstd{diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlkwb{<-} \hlstd{rosetta[rosetta[,}\hlnum{4}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
  \hlstd{\}} \hlkwa{else if} \hlstd{(diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{5}\hlstd{])\{}
    \hlstd{diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlkwb{<-} \hlstd{rosetta[rosetta[,}\hlnum{5}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_trans[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
  \hlstd{\}}
\hlstd{\}}

\hlcom{# Traduïr diff_trans_all ALERTA!!! alguns tenen multiples traduccions!}
\hlkwa{for} \hlstd{(i} \hlkwa{in} \hlnum{1}\hlopt{:}\hlkwd{length}\hlstd{(diff_trans_all[,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]))\{}
  \hlkwa{if} \hlstd{(diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{3}\hlstd{])\{}
    \hlstd{diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlkwb{<-} \hlstd{rosetta[rosetta[,}\hlnum{3}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{][}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
  \hlstd{\}} \hlkwa{else if} \hlstd{(diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{4}\hlstd{])\{}
    \hlstd{diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlkwb{<-} \hlstd{rosetta[rosetta[,}\hlnum{4}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{][}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
  \hlstd{\}} \hlkwa{else if} \hlstd{(diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{rosetta[,}\hlnum{5}\hlstd{])\{}
    \hlstd{diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlkwb{<-} \hlstd{rosetta[rosetta[,}\hlnum{5}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_trans_all[i,}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{],}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{][}\hlnum{1}\hlstd{]}
  \hlstd{\}}
\hlstd{\}}

\hlcom{#### Gens de diff_trans que estan en un o altra llista dels diffential peak callings ####}

\hlcom{# Taula}
\hlkwd{table}\hlstd{(diff_trans[,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_10G_met} \hlopt{|} \hlstd{diff_trans[,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_12B_met)}
\end{alltt}
\begin{verbatim}
## 
## FALSE  TRUE 
##    22    25
\end{verbatim}
\begin{alltt}
\hlcom{# Gens que són a la llista de diff_peaks}
\hlstd{diff_trans[diff_trans[,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_10G_met} \hlopt{|} \hlstd{diff_trans[,}\hlnum{2}\hlstd{]} \hlopt{%in%} \hlstd{diff_12B_met,]}
\end{alltt}
\begin{verbatim}
